through the following sequence:\\n\\n### 1. Service Initialization (pkg/services/ngalert/ngalert.go)\\nThe `ProvideService()` function initializes the AlertNG service, which sets up:\\n- The scheduler via `NewScheduler()` \\n- The state manager for tracking alert state transitions\\n- The alerts router for dispatching alerts\\n- The multi-org alertmanager for managing notifications\\n\\n### 2. Rule Scheduler (pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/schedule.go)\\nThe `NewScheduler()` creates the rule scheduler that:\\n- Maintains a registry of alert rules\\n- Triggers periodic evaluations based on rule intervals\\n- Manages rule lifecycle (add, update, remove)\\n- Coordinates with the state manager and alert sender\\n\\n### 3. Alert Rule Evaluation (pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/alert_rule.go)\\nThe alert rule execution flow:\\n- `newAlertRule()` creates an individual alert rule instance\\n- `alertRule.Run()` is the main evaluation loop that:\\n  - Receives evaluation signals via channel\\n  - Calls `alertRule.evaluate()` to perform the actual rule evaluation\\n  - Processes evaluation results through the state manager\\n  - Sends state transitions via `alertRule.send()`\\n\\n### 4. Condition Evaluation (pkg/services/ngalert/eval/eval.go)\\nThe evaluation factory and condition evaluator:\\n- `NewEvaluatorFactory()` creates an evaluator factory configured with datasources and expressions\\n- `EvaluatorFactory.Create()` builds a pipeline for a specific rule condition\\n- `conditionEvaluator.Evaluate()` executes the pipeline against datasources and returns raw results\\n- Results are converted to alert instances with labels and annotations\\n\\n### 5. State Management (pkg/services/ngalert/state/manager.go, pkg/services/ngalert/state/state.go)\\nState transitions are managed through:\\n- `NewManager()` creates the state manager with persistence and historian backends\\n- `Manager.ProcessEvalResults()` processes evaluation results and:\\n  - Creates/updates State objects for each alert instance\\n  - Determines state transitions (Normal → Alerting, Alerting → Resolved, etc.)\\n  - Records transitions to historians for audit/history\\n  - Filters which states need to be sent based on `NeedsSending()` logic\\n  - Calls the sender callback with StateTransitions to dispatch\\n\\n### 6. Internal Notification Dispatch (pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/alertmanager.go, multiorg_alertmanager.go)\\nInternal alertmanager processing:\\n- `MultiOrgAlertmanager.AlertmanagerFor()` retrieves the alertmanager instance for an organization\\n- `alertmanager.PutAlerts()` receives alerts and forwards to the underlying GrafanaAlertmanager\\n- The alertmanager applies the organization's routing rules and notification policies\\n\\n### 8. Receiver Service (pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/receiver_svc.go)\\nThe ReceiverService manages:\\n- Receiver configuration and lifecycle\\n- Routing decisions based on alert labels\\n- Integration with notification channels (email, webhook, Slack, etc.)\\n- Access control for receiver management\\n\\n### External Alertmanagers (pkg/services/ngalert/sender/sender.go)\\nFor external alertmanager routing:\\n- `ExternalAlertmanager` manages connections to external Alertmanager instances\\n- Uses service discovery to discover and route to external Alertmanager replicas\\n- Implements batch queueing and retries for reliable delivery\\n\\n## Key Data Flow\\n\\n1. **Scheduler tick** → Rule evaluation requested\\n2. **Rule evaluation** → Condition queries datasources via expression service\\n3. **Results processing** → State manager transitions states based on results\\n4. **Alert dispatch** → Router sends alerts to internal/external notifiers\\n5. **Notification routing** → Alertmanager applies routing rules to receivers\\n6. **Receiver dispatch** → Notifications sent to configured channels (email, webhook, etc.)\\n\\nThe entire flow is instrumented with tracing (OpenTelemetry) and metrics for observability, and supports features like alert silencing, state persistence, and audit history.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":8,"cache_creation_input_tokens":350,"cache_read_input_tokens":72150,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":350},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"9b25a9aa-7200-4f6a-ac17-3886c09ff260","uuid":"f6c1bd3c-ecce-45ec-b24d-c90b47502b7e"}

Alert Rule Evaluation (pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/alert_rule.go)\\nThe alert rule execution flow:\\n- `newAlertRule()` creates an individual alert rule instance\\n- `alertRule.Run()` is the main evaluation loop that:\\n  - Receives evaluation signals via channel\\n  - Calls `alertRule.evaluate()` to perform the actual rule evaluation\\n  - Processes evaluation results through the state manager\\n  - Sends state transitions via `alertRule.send()`\\n\\n### 4. Condition Evaluation (pkg/services/ngalert/eval/eval.go)\\nThe evaluation factory and condition evaluator:\\n- `NewEvaluatorFactory()` creates an evaluator factory configured with datasources and expressions\\n- `EvaluatorFactory.Create()` builds a pipeline for a specific rule condition\\n- `conditionEvaluator.Evaluate()` executes the pipeline against datasources and returns raw results\\n- Results are converted to alert instances with labels and annotations\\n\\n### 5. queueing and retries for reliable delivery\\n\\n## Key Data Flow\\n\\n1. **Scheduler tick** → Rule evaluation requested\\n2. **Rule evaluation** → Condition queries datasources via expression service\\n3. **Results processing** → State manager transitions states based on results\\n4. **Alert dispatch** → Router sends alerts to internal/external notifiers\\n5. **Notification routing** → Alertmanager applies routing rules to receivers\\n6. **Receiver dispatch** → Notifications sent to configured channels (email, webhook, etc.)\\n\\nThe entire flow is instrumented with tracing (OpenTelemetry) and metrics for observability, and supports features like alert silencing, state persistence, and audit
